 gaja ko haalanki jald hi safalataa mil gai jab unhone shreyas ayyar ko wicketiper parthiv ke haathon kaich karaayaa

 is yuva ballebaaj ne hardik patel par gendbaaj ke sir ke upar se chakka lagaaya lekin agali gend par ek ran churaane ke prayaas main vah ran out ho gaye

 Car sales in India declined partially in May as demand for utility vehicles (UV) increased slightly compared to the sedan recently, while sales of entry-level hatchbacks are being affected in view of the softening in rural markets
 sosayadi of indian automobile manuphactures (siam) dwaara jari aankadon ke mutabik may main 1,58,996 kaaron kii bikri hui jo pichley saal ke isi maheene main 1,60,371 ikai thi
 Siam Director General Vishnu Mathur said, "car sales declined slightly last month as the utility vehicle segment, instead of sedans, grew slightly due to the introduction of several new compact suvs

 Ranatunga, one of the outspoken critics of the IPL, expressed surprise that many great cricketers are speaking in favor of the IPL
 unhone kaha, mujhe dukh he ki apane jamaane ke kai mahaan cricketer paisa kamaane ke liye ipel kaa bachaav kar rahe hai
 There are only a few cricketers like Irapalli Prasanna, who have come out openly against it
 unhone kaha, ipel kyon khelaa ja rahaa he
 What has Indian cricket got from this? vishwa cricket main bharat kii itani badanaami kabhi nahin hui
 It is a case equivalent to the 2000 match-fixing episode and its impact is not limited to India alone
 rantunga ne kaha, mujhe pichley chah saal main ek bhi khilaadi aisa nahin dekha jo bhartiya cricket ko ipel kii dein ho
 Due to the IPL, India will never get players like Tendulkar, Dravid, Gavaskar or Kapil
 unhone yah bhi kaha ki bisisiai kaa gharelu cricket kaa dhaancha itnaa sakasham he ki usase achche cricketer nikal sake or use ipel kii koi jarurat nahin he
 He also said that corruption has been suspected not just in IPL 6 but in every session and that Sir Pal Kandon, the former chairman of the ICC anti-corruption Unit, hinted at it only after the first session of IPL in 2008
 rantunga ne kaha, ipel main phixing kaa khulaasa ab hua he, lekin 2008 main pehle satr se hi shaq kii sui is lig par thi
 Sir Pal Kandon also gave a document on this to the ICC Board
 unhone kaha, sar paal condon ne kaha tha ki nabbe ke dashak ke baad ab ipel cricket main bhrashtachar ke aasaan jariye ke rup main ubhara he
 If BCCI really had to remove corruption from cricket, then action should have been taken at that time
 unhone kaha, lekin bhartiya board ne apni khud kii bhrashtachar nirodhak ikai banaai or har ipel main koi naa koi vivaad judaa rahaa
 It is not cricket but the spectacle of cricket and making players greedy
 tippaniyan Asked about reports of some Indian bookies being the benami owners of some franchises in the Sri Lanka Premier League, Ranatunga said it should be investigated
 unhone kaha, maine bhi aisi khabaren padhi hai
 i was also against the Sri Lanka Premier League from the beginning, because i was afraid that with any such league, non-essential things would also come into cricket
 agar aisa he to isaki jaanch honi chahie
 Ranatunga also said that there should be an independent inquiry into irregularities in the IPL and the government should interfere in it
 unhone kaha, bharat sarkaar ko chahie ki bisisiai ko apni chhatrachhaaya main le jaisaa ki srilanka main he
 The current BCCI office bearers should be sacked and re-elected
 rantunga ne kaha, main pehle se kahata aayaa hum ki ipel cricket main sattebaaji, phixing, sharabkhori, doping jaisi kai buraaiyon ko lekar aayaa he
 The current spot-fixing episode has served to strike the last nail in the coffin and i believe the IPL should be discontinued for the betterment of cricket
 ipel ke mukhar aalochakon main se ek rahe rantunga ne hairaani jataai ki kai mahaan cricketer ipel ke paksh main bol rahe hai
 He said, i am sad that many great cricketers of his day are defending IPL to make money
 irapalli prasanna jaise kuch hi cricketer hai, jo iske khilaaf khulkar saamne aae hai
 He said, why is the IPL being played
 isse bhartiya cricket ko kya mila he
 India has never been so infamous in world cricket
 yah 2000 ke match phixing prakaran ke baraabar kaa maamla he or iskaa asar sirf bharat tak simit nahin he
 Ranatunga said, "I have not seen a single player in the last six years who owes IPL to Indian cricket
" ipel ke chalate bharat ko kabhi tendulkar, dravid, gavaskar yaa kapil jaise khilaadi nahin mil sakenge
 He also said that the bcci's structure of domestic cricket is so capable that it can produce good cricketers and there is no need of IPL
 unhone yah bhi kaha ki sirf ipel chah hi nahin balki har satr main bhrashtachar kaa shaq rahaa he or isisi kii bhrashtachar nirodhak ikai ke purv adhyaksh sar paal condon ne 2008 main ipel ke pehle satr ke baad hi iske sanket die the

 Rangoli art has different names in different states in India
 uttar pradesh main ise chowk poorna kaha jaataa he, rajasthan main ise mandana, bihar main aripan, pashchim bengal main alpana, maharashtra main rangoli, karnataka main rangavelli, andhrapradesh main muggu yaa muggulu, himachal pradesh main arupan, kumau main alikhthaap yaa thapa or gujarat main saathiyo kaha jaataa he
 Rangoli is made in the morning in front of the main gate in Maharashtra
 manyata he ki dwaar par saji rangoli buree takat ko andar aane se rokatii he
 Kerala has a tradition of making Onam Rangoli for years
 olym parv par banaai jane vaali is rangoli main phulon kii pankhudiyon kaa istemaal kiya jaataa he
 Nowadays this trend is seen in other states as well

 Then it is filled with color

 yahaan rangoli kaa yah rup alikhthaap kehalaata he

 chaukor khaane vaali saathiyo ko ‚Äòchakda‚Äô kaha jaataa he
 Interestingly, in South India, where Rangoli is based on geometric shapes, while making Rangoli in North India, auspicious symbols like Swastik, Om are made

 rangoli kaa koi nishchit rup nahin hota

 ise deepon se bhi sajaayaa jaataa he

 iske liye tel rangon kaa istemaal kiya jaataa he
